info:Deluxe Room - Garden-View (2 beds)
info:Stayed in June 2024
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:2.2
posted:Posted June 10, 2024
msg:Breakfast was 5 star. Furnishings and exterior was 5 star. 
It costs CNY40-60 to travel to the city, or CNY100 if the hotel arranges it for you. 
Perhaps due to low occupancy, there was only 1 staff at the reception, handling phone calls and requests from guests. 
Amenities are mainly for children. Gym closes at 5pm, and there's nothing much to do in the hotel if you're not a parent with children. 
The compound engages a security guard to prevent non-guests from entering and using their facilities. But guests get stopped and questioned; sometimes taxis booked by guests are delayed as they are not allowed to drive into the compound which the main lobby is, creating additional hassle of having to inform the driver to phone the hotel. 
It is a hotel with big ambitions (several areas still under development) and lavish furnishings (every piece of furniture looks expensive). Unlike advertised on Trip, there was no peacock show. A few peacocks roamed around freely. Complimentary milk and dessert is a small tetra pack milk and a packet of dates.

The waiters are very friendly and enthusiastic. The only shortcoming is that the room is not soundproof. Because most of the guests are families and children, the children are very noisy at night.
